```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
```
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
```dafny
}

// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
```
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

  decreases |s|

}

The original program (without assertions) is:

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

```dafny
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
```
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}
```

  decreases |s|

```dafny
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
```
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}
```

ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {
    i := i - 1;
  }
  // After the loop, i is the index of the last non-')' character
  // or -1 if the whole string consists of ')'.
  // Therefore TrailingParens(s[..i+1]) == 0.
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;

```dafny
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{

    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1

    i := i - 1;
```

ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {
    i := i - 1;
  }

  // After the loop, i is either -1 or the index of the first non-')' from the end.
  // Therefore the substring s[..i+1] contains no trailing ')'.
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;

  // The number of trailing ')' characters is |s| - (i + 1).
  var trailing := |s| - (i + 1);
  // The number of remaining characters is |s| - trailing.
  var remaining := |s| - trailing;
  bad := trailing > remaining;
}

ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {
    i := i - 1;
  }

  // After the loop, i is the index of the first character that is not ')'
  // or -1 if all characters are ')'.  The substring s[..i+1] contains
  // exactly the non-trailing part of the string, so its TrailingParens
  // value must be 0.
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;

  // x is the number of trailing ')' characters.
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}
